 1
 Identity: The man is neither high, nor low, nor big, nor small
 aadmi sirf aadmi hota he
 Do not know why this straightforward truth does not know Kodunia? And if it does not know, then why does it not matter with the mind that it does not matter where the man is standing? On the path or on the chariot? On the arrow or on the ramparts
 Where is the ground, or where he has to stand, what is his surface? Unfaithful to, then what will be Apradislia forgivable was at an altitude of Kivh Everest? No offense offense will remain, the Himalayas may not cover all Dhavltaus sunburn
 kapadon kii dudhia safedi jaiseman kii malinta ko nahin chipa sakati
 Some saint poet has said that no one is above human beings, i think he has a mind over a human being
 chote man se koi bada nahin hota,toote man se koi khadaa nahin hota
 That is why Lord Krishna was decorated with weapons, climbed the chariot, Arjuna had to recite the Gita while standing in the Kurukshetra field
 man harkar, maidan nahin jite jate,na maidan jeetne se man hi jite jate hai
 Falling from the peak causes more injury
 asthi jud jaati,pidaa man main sulagati he
 This does not mean not only to challenge the climb, but it also does not mean that you are not determined to conquer the situation
 aadmi jahaan he, vahiin khadaa rahe?dusron kii dayaa ke bharose par padaa rahe?jadta kaa naam jivan nahin he,palaayan purogaman nahin he
 a man should fight with extreme circumstances, one dream is broken and another is fabricated
 kintu kitna bhi ooncha uthe,manushyata ke str se na gire,apane dharaatal ko na chode,antaryami se munh na mode

 padhie atal kii wo kavita

 2
 On the high mountain, trees do not grow, plants do not grow, nor grass is stored
 jamati he sirf barf,jo, kafan kii tarah safed or,maut kii tarah thandi hoti he

 oonchai or gaharaai menakash-pataal kii duuri he

 zaruri yah he kioonchai ke saath vistaar bhi ho,jisase manushya,thunth sa khadaa na rahe,auron se ghule-mili,kisi ko saath le,kisi ke sang chale

 dharti ko bunon kii nahin,oonche kad ke insaanon kii jarurat he

 gurjar sarkari naukariyon main paanch pratishat aarakshan kii maang ko lekar pradarshan kar rahe hai
 a single bench of the court said, AAP (chief Secretary and DGP) being the head of bureaucracy and law and order machinery, is not bound to remain a mere spectator of political dialogue between the Gurjar protesters and the state government
 nyaayamurti ares rathod ne kaha, ham in aloktantric pradarshnon se logon ko mushkil main daalane kii anumati nahin de sakate
 It seems that both of you have become insensitive to the problems of common people
 ham spasht shabdon main aapse yah kah rahe hai ki adaalat yah dekhnaa chaahati he ki avarodhakon ko aaj tatkaal hataaya jaae or rail path evam rajmarg ko raatbhar awajahi ke liye saaf kiya jaae or jab ham yah kah rahe hai to hamen gambhirtha se liya janaa chahie
 The order came in connection with a contempt petition pending since 2008 against Gurjar leaders, including Colonel Kirori S
 Bainsla, for violation of High Court orders

 The court also expressed displeasure over the inaction of the chief security officer of RPF in preventing the protesters from removing the fish plates from the rail tracks in the affected areas
 iske kaaran dilli or jaipur ke bich rail yatayaat baadhit ho gaya he
 Justice Rathore said, the state administration has lodged an FIR under stringent provisions for waging war against the state, but not a single nominated person has been arrested nor investigation has been initiated
 isse purv gurjar netaaon or sarkaar ke bich buudhvaar ko chauthe daur kii baatcheet main bhi samaadhaan nahin niklaa
 Parliamentary Affairs Minister Rajendra Rathod, a member of the three-member cabinet sub-committee, dismissed the demand of Gurjar agitators outrightly after the fourth round of negotiations ended, giving five percent reservation to Gujjars within fifty percent of social harmony
 Damage can be reached
 sarkaar ko ummid he ki gurjar aandolankaaree masaude par vichaar karne ke baad agle daur kii baatcheet karenge
 The three-member cabinet sub-committee includes Parliamentary Affairs Minister Rajendra Rathore, Social Justice and Empowerment Minister Dr
 Arun Chaturvedi and Food and Civil Supplies Minister Hem Singh Bhadana
 tippaniyan Himmat Singh, a spokesperson of the Rajasthan Gurjar Reservation Sangharsh Samiti and involved in talks with the government, said that we did not agree on the draft given by the government during the fourth round of talks, we need only five percent reservation within the purview of fifty percent reservation
 gauratlab he ki rajasthan gurjar aarakshan sangharsh samiti maujuuda samay pachaas pratishat aarakshan ke daayre main gurjaron ko paanch pratishat aarakshan dene kii maang kar rahi he
 Presently, the Gujjars are getting one percent reservation in the range of fifty percent and they demand that it be reduced to five percent
 baaki bache chaar pratishat aarakshan dene kaa maamla ucch nyaayalay main lambit he
 Roads and rail services have been disrupted in the state due to the protests by Gurjars, due to which the common people are facing a lot of problems
 hoicourt ne adhikariyon se kaha ki ve sabhi sadakon or rail margon se avrodh hataane ke liye tatkaal karrwai karen
 The court directed the Chief Secretary and the DGP to submit an affidavit till yesterday to explain why action was not taken against the protesters under the FIR registered
 adaalat ne unase kaha ki ve gurjaron ke virodh-pradarshan ke kaaran nijee evam saarvajanik sampatti ko hue nuksaan kii vistrut jaankaree muhaiyaa karaaen
 Gurjars are demonstrating demanding five percent reservation in government jobs
 adaalat kii ekal peeth ne kaha, aap (mukhya sachiv or dijipi) naukarshahi or kanoon vyavastha tantra ke pramukh hone ke naate gurjar pradarshnakariyon or rajya sarkaar ke bich raajnneetik vaarta ke keval darshak bane rahane ke liye baadhya nahin hai
 Justice RS Rathore said, "we cannot allow these undemocratic demonstrations to trouble people
" aisa prathit hota he ki aap donon aam logon kii mushkilon ko lekar samvedanheen ho gaye hai
 We are telling you clearly that the court wants to see that the blockers are removed immediately and the railroad and highway be cleared for overnight movement and we should be taken seriously when we are saying this
 yah aadesh ucch nyaayalay ke adeshon ke ulanghan ko lekar karnal kirodi es bansla samet gurjar netaaon ke khilaaf 2008 se lambit avmaananaa yachika ke sambandh main aayaa he
 The DRM of the Railway Department and the Chief Security Officer of the Railway Police Force (RPF) in Kota division were also present in the court
 adaalat ne prabhavit ilaakon main pradarshnakariyon ko rail patariyon se fish plate hataane se rokane main arpeef ke mukhya suraksha adhikari kii niskriyata par bhi nakhushi jataai
 This has disrupted rail traffic between Delhi and Jaipur
 nyaayamurti rathod ne kaha, rajya prashasan ne rajya ke khilaaf yuddh chhedane ke liye kade praavdhaanon ke tahat praathmiki darj kii he, lekin ek bhi namjad vyakti ko giraftaar nahin kiya gaya he or na hi jaanch shuru kii gai he
 Earlier, in the fourth round of talks between the Gurjar leaders and the government on Wednesday, no solution was found
 teen sadasyeey mantrimandal up samiti ke sadsy sansadeey kaary mantri rajendra rathod ne chauthe daur kii baatcheet samaapt hone ke baad gurjar aandolankariyon kii maang ko sire se khaarij karte hue do took main kaha, pachaas fisadi ke bheetar gurjaron ko paanch pratishat aarakshan dene se saamaajik samarasata ko nuksaan panhuch saktaa he
 The government hopes that the Gujjars will discuss the next round after considering the agitational draft
 teen sadasyeey mantrimandaleey up samiti main sansadeey kaary mantri rajendra rathod ,saamaajik nyaay evam adhikarita mantri da arun chaturvedi or khaadya env naagarik aapurti mantri hem singh bhadana shaamil hai
 The comments rajasthan gurjar aarakshan sangharsh samiti ke pravaktaa or sarkaar se baatcheet main shaamil himmat singh ne kaha ki sarkaar dwaara chauthe daur kii baatcheet ke dauraan die gaye masaude par sahamat nahin hai, hamen pachaas pratishat aarakshan ke daayre main hi paanch pratishat aarakshan chahie
 It is worth noting that Rajasthan Gurjar Reservation Sangharsh Samiti is currently demanding five percent reservation for Gurjars under the purview of fifty percent reservation
 vartmaan main gurjaron ko pachaas pratishat ke daayre main ek pratishat aarakshan mil rahaa he or unki maang he ki ise paanch pratishat kiya jaae
 The matter of giving the remaining four percent reservation is pending in the High Court
